void urlDecode(char *src, char *dst) {
 char a, b;
 while (*src) {
 if ((*src == '%') &&
 ((a = src[1]) && (b = src[2])) &&
 (isxdigit(a) && isxdigit(b))) {
 if (a >= 'a')
 a -= 'a'-'A';
 if (a >= 'A')
 a -= ('A' - 10);
 else
 a -= '0';
 if (b >= 'a')
 b -= 'a'-'A';
 if (b >= 'A')
 b -= ('A' - 10);
 else
 b -= '0';
 *dst++ = 16*a+b;
 src+=3;
 } else {
 *dst++ = *src++;
 }
 }
 *dst++ = '\0';
}
int isValid(char *src) {
 int i = 0;
 while (src[i] != '\0') {
 if(src[i] == ';') {
 if (i == 0 || src[i-1] != '\\') {
 return 0;
 }
 }
 else if(src[i] == '|') {
 if (i == 0 || src[i-1] != '\\') {
 return 0;
 }
 }
 else if(src[i] == '&') {
 if (i == 0 || src[i-1] != '\\') {
 return 0;
 }
 }
 i++;
 }
 return 1;
}
